You need read comments in the POC first.

My Test machine specifications are:
    MacBook Pro (Retina, 13-inch, Early 2015)
    Processor  2.7 GHz Intel Core i5
    Memory     8 GB 1867 MHz DDR3
    Graphics    Intel Iris Graphics 6100 1536 MB

POC is based on System loaded IOHIDDevice. So
1, you may need to find one IOHIDDevice with bigger MaxInputReportSize on your test machine. If POC not crash under kernel.development.
2, Get a element with input report from the IOHIDDevice, and ReportSize of the element is bigger than max(_maxOutputReportSize, _maxFeatureReportSize)
3, Get the cookie of the element.


For example, There is one IOHIDDevice description found from output of ioreg -lxf:
